mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">I am posting this blog on specific request from a reader Dhruv\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">In 1986, my ship was one of the first foreign ships to berth at China , who had just opened her Bamboo doors. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>My ship drydocked at Quindao . The yard threw a great 30 course dinner. The Chairman of the yard , a past weightlifting champion of China , was constantly trying to engage me in a drinking contest. And to be polite I played ball ( more on getting arm twisted by the rest of my officers and the company Suptd ).<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">I was pretty sozzled, as I was NOT a great drinker. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Even then I noted a man sitting next to the Chairman , who was looking extremely uncomfortable, and was silent. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>So I asked the translator, who is this corny guy? <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He whispered into my ear that he was the chauffer of the Chairman, and both of them nearly got the same salary. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>If the driver of his car was NOT treated the same , the communist party politburo might ask for an explanation, the next day. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>And the chairman would NOT even know if the silent guy was a party Commissar spy.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Same way in communist Russia, a brain dead stupid man would get the same salary as a genius like IE Irodov ( All IIT guys know who this great Physics professor was ). Such was the communist system. To keep such a abnormal system alive there has to be ironhanded rule. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Democracy will NOT allow a donkey to be treated the same as a race horse on the track, or vice versa on a Dhobi ghat. One of them will have more value.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">God has NOT created everybody the same.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Firstly he made man and woman . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">No matter how much a woman says she is equal to man , she cannot be . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">If any woman disagrees, please point out one animal or bird or mammal where the female gender is more intelligent, beautiful or stronger than the male gender ( insects please excuse ). <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Male Olympics records are better that that of the female category. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>A master tailor is a man. A master cook is a man. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Almost all inventions have been made by man.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Same way , among men \u2014 all are NOT equal. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Some are more intelligent, some are more handsome and some are more stronger . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">This is the way reality is. There is NO point in bitching about it.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">So if you are Bill Gates, running a software company, you will NOT show too much sentiments like the Govt of India and have a quota for the lesser category. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">And if you were the Captain of the Indian cricket team, you will NOT agree to have a physically challenged man in your team , out of sentiments.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Or if you are the producer of a movie you will NOT have a Mayawati type as your heroine. The male audience is supposed to see her at night in their wet dreams.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">In any Univeristy, the intellectual cream gets computer science, the less intelligent category gets governmental studies , textile engineering or its ilk. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">My son who passed out of Cornell USA , sat in his Computers class room on the first day and got a surprise. There were hardly anyone of the superior white category , like what you get to see in the same college canteen. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This computer classroom has <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Indians, Chinese, Koreans , dirty pariah whites, plus a sprinking of English speaking superior whites. There was NOT a single black American . It was all about grey matter.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Same way, 8000 years back our Vedic system has a Chaturvarna system. Those days the population was few. There was NO need for present day exam system, as there were superior people with 12 strand DNA who could judge your intrinsic worth just by looking at your physical aura.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Since 2000 BC, there has been NO Maharishi superhumans of Brahmin class born with 12 strand DNA. This is due to lack of cosmic rays and star dust. The degraded Brahmin class could NOT do wonders , which would earn instant respect. This meant that respect had to be earned.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">So the Vedic Sanatana Dharma system has the 4 classes, or graded inequality to sustain society. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Brahmins, Kshatriyas, Vaishyas and Shudras . The Muslims who invaded India called the local population Hindus.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: x-large;\">The picture below gives some propaganda.&nbsp; <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">These words are&nbsp;NOT there in the original Vedas</span>.&nbsp; <span style=\"color: red;\">This Shudras being from the feet etc -- is all bullshit</span> .&nbsp; <span style=\"color: blue;\">This&nbsp;was added by the clever Brahmins , to cheat the public -- that there have been given powers over the rest by divinity.</span></span> </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tPdHDgURjxU/TicZFI20cgI/AAAAAAAAEKE/aZnCKTIW1Sw/s1600/imagesCA4VL7QN.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"298\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tPdHDgURjxU/TicZFI20cgI/AAAAAAAAEKE/aZnCKTIW1Sw/s400/imagesCA4VL7QN.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><strong>THE NOBLE VEDIC <span style=\"background-color: lime; font-size: x-large;\">&nbsp;\"&nbsp;TEAM DYNAMICS\" </span>&nbsp;SYSTEM GOT CORRUPTED , BY THE DIVIDE AND RULE INVADER POLICIES-- </strong></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em>To understand this TEAM DYNAMICS concept-- </em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em>can you build a skyscraper by a bunch of architects alone? -- </em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em>or a bunch of masons alone?&nbsp; or a bunch of musclemen?&nbsp;&nbsp; </em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em>or a bunch of climbers who are NOT afraid of heights? --&nbsp; </em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em>NO --all are interdependant, &nbsp;like a ship's crew list. It is the diversity of the team which causes it to produce magic.</em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;; font-size: large;\"><em>This does NOT mean that the captain can shit on the faces of the lower rung crew!&nbsp;&nbsp; Or&nbsp;architects can shit on the faces of the masons and musclemen. &nbsp;Or forwards in a soccer team shitting on the defenders . If they do so, they are exceeding their team dynamics &nbsp;brief and natural justice must be invoked.</em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><strong>THIS IS WHAT IT GOT REDUCED TO -- IN A PATHETIC MANNER -- <span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\">BY DIVIDE AND RULE POLICIES OF OUR INVADERS --</span></strong></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">The Brahmins' occupation was to learn, teach and officiate at religious ceremonies. They were supposed to be brainy. They would sit in the current day Computer science class. They could learn and teach and officiate. <o:p></o:p></span></em></span></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">The Kshatriyas' occupation was to bear arms and to fight. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>They were supposed to be firm limbed. These are the ones who would be in the line up for a Olympic Marathon race or a boxing contest. Kings came from this category.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">The occupation of the Vaishyas was trade and business. They were the talented people. They could be called the skilled workers , craftsmen and traders.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></span></div>\n<em style=\"color: blue; font-family: Calibri;\">The Shudras' occupation was to do physical work and menial service. They did NOT measure up to the top three. Like in every beauty contest, the ones who don\u2019t measure up will be eliminated in the first preliminary. They can hardly bitch about it\u2014.</em><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iwPmMVMOTy0/TicZRcbUypI/AAAAAAAAEKI/WoQYQhUmrJk/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iwPmMVMOTy0/TicZRcbUypI/AAAAAAAAEKI/WoQYQhUmrJk/s320/untitled.png\" width=\"236\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Ayurvedic word for toxins, ama, means, \"crude\" or \"raw\" - residues from faulty or incomplete pepsis that haven't been properly integrated into the body and its functioning, and therefore impede it.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">OK, FOLKS, TIMES HAS NOW COME TO BUST A BOMBSHELL WHICH IS GONNA SHIVER YOUR TIMBERS&nbsp;&nbsp;.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Enter Orpheus&nbsp;&nbsp;\u2013&nbsp;&nbsp;the Indian seer , a master musician and sitarist,&nbsp;&nbsp;the holy man who brought Pythagoras to Kerala by ship and took him back via Muzris ( Kodungallur\u2014 cultural centre of Calicut king&nbsp;&nbsp;) Bernice&nbsp;&nbsp;( Red sea port of Egypt ) and Alexandria ( Egypt ) .&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Orpheus was a Brahmachari , a celebate sage who was a veena virtuoso.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Veena is the oldest musical instrument on the planet.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Jealous Aristotle and Plato tried to paint him as a homosexual and a woman hater, which he was NOT.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Herodotus had clearly written that Orpheus who would play divine string music and tame wild animals came from India.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Orpheus , a strict vegetarian introduced spirituality to Greece&nbsp;&nbsp;.&nbsp;&nbsp;He was known for the use of holy theertham from a copper bowl and a Tulsi ( basil) leaf which he used to keep in his mouth .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Cicero called Orpheus , the tawny hued , a devotee of Bacchus ( Krishna ) crowned with kissos ( Tulsi).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Western historians and the Pope blurred&nbsp;&nbsp;Jesus and Orpheus , and pretty soon it was Jesus who was attributed to all the qualities of Orpheus \u2013 enchanting wild animals with a 7 stringed lyre .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The original sitar ( derived from the veena&nbsp;&nbsp;) has seven strings&nbsp;&nbsp;which run over curved, raised frets ( Rudra / Saraswati veena) , and the remainder are sympathetic strings (tarb,&nbsp;&nbsp;taarif , tarafdaar) which run underneath the frets and resonate in sympathy with the played strings.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">It was Orpheus who gave Pythagoras&nbsp;&nbsp;the mathematical relations of the notes on the musical scale.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The wisdom of the ancients has been taught by the philosophers of Greece, but also by people called Jews in Syria, and by Brahmins in India.\"--Megasthenes- 300 BC.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Orpheus the tawny hued Hindu Maharishi from Kerala, India gave music to the west.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Before that their music consisted of clanging rocks and shouting nonsense. .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Orpheus also gave&nbsp;&nbsp;astrology and magic ( mantravadam ),&nbsp;&nbsp;vedic metaphysics ( magna grecia ) from Kerala to the west.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Orpheus was a master in astrology, and all Greek astrology is though Orpheus.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Greeks spliced on the FAKE story of Eurydice to Orpheus, based on the MIRRORED version of ancient Hindu myth of Savitri and Satyavan.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">This is about the efforts of Orpheus to retrieve his wife, Eurydice, (who was killed by a serpent on their wedding night ) from the underworld. Orpheus went down to Hades to claim her, and played so sweetly with his lute that Pluto allowed Eurydice to return to the earth with Orpheus, but on condition that he did not look behind him until he had reached the terrestrial regions. Orpheus, however, in his anxiety to see if she were following him, looked round, and Eurydice disappeared from his sight, instantly and forever.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">This LOOKING BACK story is mirrored from the lore of Adi Shankaracharya bringing Devi to Kerala in 2000 BC \u2014&nbsp;&nbsp;he looked back and Devi disappeared at the spot of Mookambika temple at Kollur Karnataka.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Pythagoras learnt metempsychosis from India.&nbsp;&nbsp;Metempsychosis is the Greek equivalent of the 11000 year old Vedic Hindu doctrine of transmigration of the soul, Karma and and reincarnation after death.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Almost every Greek text tells that Orpheos was famous for Ahimsa or non-violence . In Euripides' play Hippolytos a father taunts his son with the \"lifeless food\" he eats since taking Orpheos for his \"king.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Orpheus is praised for his knowledge of medicine and astrology ( ONLY Ayurveda and Indian astrology existed those days).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Punch into Google search-<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>MIHIRA MUNI , THE GREAT ASTROLOGER CUM ASTRONOMER VADAKAYIL</b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The name of India, so far as is known, first appears in Greek literature in the 5th century B.C. in the works of Hekataios and Herodotos.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Herodotos of Halikarnassos (484-425 B. C.) whose histories have survived in their entirety had written clearly about India .&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Herodotos writes about India's population, saying that the Indians are \"more in number than any nation known to me.\u201d&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">He goes to great details while telling of Kerala\u2019s&nbsp;&nbsp;wealth in gold; He tells about&nbsp;&nbsp;Indian birds and beasts he regards as much bigger than those existing elsewhere, except for horses. Indian clothing he describes as made from wool growing on trees (i.e. cotton) and the amazing thin cotton Calico cloth , we use in Kerala as Mundu ( dhoti ).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Herodotos' most famous statement about India- that gold is produced in the Indian desert by fierce ants larger than foxes- , which appears to be bull, just for kicks.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Unless these large ants were golden jackals who would call a nearby tiger .&nbsp;&nbsp;Such jackals had terrific night vision and sniffing ability ( excellent for bomb detection squads ) and leads the tiger to juicy prey , and then eats the left overs , which the grateful tiger deliberately leave behind.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Many Indian seers visited Greece , as in 7000 BC, India ruled Palistan ( Palestine ) . Once when Socrates was asked by an Indian seer, what he does for a living . When Socrates replied that he \"investigated human life,\" the Indian laughed aloud , saying that \"no one was able to observe human affairs if he was ignorant of divine matters and consciousness .\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Vegetarianism in Greece is called Orphikos bios, or \"Orphic way of life\". Only Indians were vegetarians those days.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Aristotle ran down OR rather tried to convert Orpheus to be a homosexual like him, just because of a song he wrote about a red-lipped boy on the ship Argos. ( AAHA red lips&nbsp;&nbsp;came out of sucking too hard TEE HEEEE )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Both Orpeheus and the converted Pythagoras forbade the sacrifice of animals\u2014so there goes the western theory of animal sacrifice in Indian temples.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Let me quote ( I usually do NOT care for such third party references ) of the parallels between the Orphic path and the yogic as written by Joseph John Campbell :&nbsp;&nbsp;\u201ca system both of thought and practice, exactly paralleling that of Indian asceticism, was communicated by initiated masters to little circles of devotees.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The soul, it was declared, returned repeatedly to life, bound to the wheel of rebirth (compare the Sanskrit samsara).&nbsp;&nbsp;Through asceticism (Sanskrit, tapas), however, the body could be purged of its Titan dross (Sanskrit, mirjara, \u2018shedding\u2019) and the soul released (Sanskrit, moksha, \u2018release\u2019).&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Also, rituals fostering meditation on the godly factor were of help (Sanskrit, bhakti, \u2018devotion\u2019).&nbsp;&nbsp;And when, at last, in rapture (samadhi), the initiate cleaved to his own intrinsic being (svasvarupman), he was divine (Shivaham, \u2018I am Shiva.\u2019)\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The gay side kick of Aristotle wrote : \u201c Orpheus so hated women he chose to be reborn as a motherless swan\u201d&nbsp;&nbsp;.&nbsp;&nbsp;It is a pity that he visited India , yet he knew nothing of Brahmacharya.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">However Plato respects Orpheus for his poetry ,the sweet hymns&nbsp;&nbsp;of the hexameter form that revolutionized Greek poetry.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For Greek / Latin classics Homer's Iliad and Odyssey and Virgil's Aeneid have inherent the Dactylic hexameter ( heroic hexameter)&nbsp;&nbsp;a form of meter in poetry or a rhythmic scheme, like the metered Sanskrit verses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The mysterious The Testament of Orpheus was the most important Orphic document for six centuries after it\u2019s \u201cdiscovery\u201d circa 300 AD.&nbsp;&nbsp;In it Orpheus says when in Egypt he met Moses who taught him about monotheism.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A circa 350 AD hematite magic amulet, once in the collection of the Berlin Museum, depicted a man crucified on a cross with a moon and seven stars above his head and the words Orpheoc Bakkikoc.&nbsp;&nbsp;It was declared to be a forgery by a furious pope Pius XII.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Orphic doctrine was purely vedic Indian and&nbsp;&nbsp;remained on a mythological plane, interpreting the universe in terms of personalized deities and procreation. Pythagoras refined and rationalized it and grabbed the glory later.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A Indian Christian trader named Theophilos, from originally from Kerala and resident in Socotra island ( Aloe vera trade ) undertook several missionary journeys on behalf of the Roman emperor Constantius in the mid-4th century.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;He writes of a small Christian community in on the Malabar coast which traces its origins to Jesus' disciples Thomas and&nbsp;&nbsp;Bartholomew.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; however, each time he is named in the company of Philip.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "12", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/5964370805133399690/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "3593303722039745083", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-07-19T08:28:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-08-22T12:36:37+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTM0OTIxNTk3MDQxCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/07/unlearning-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/3593303722039745083", "title": "UNLEARNING -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JX9Go-GiRSU/TiTvWtAdAQI/AAAAAAAAEBk/q54vJvZJyqI/s1600/PA260003.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JX9Go-GiRSU/TiTvWtAdAQI/AAAAAAAAEBk/q54vJvZJyqI/s320/PA260003.JPG\" width=\"286\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">When my elder son passed out of Cornell with a valuable ME in computer science, and got a plum job in one of the best paying computer software companies of USA, my only words of advise to him , was this ancient Indian Vedic wisdom.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-AzJeDXyTR44/TiZPVuBVHbI/AAAAAAAAEFM/NbhRYu-tt50/s1600/imagesCA3Z3KSY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-AzJeDXyTR44/TiZPVuBVHbI/AAAAAAAAEFM/NbhRYu-tt50/s320/imagesCA3Z3KSY.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>\u201c Son, truth is a pathless land. You will need to free yourself from the usual conditioned responses. The process of unlearning, and shedding obsolete snakeskins , <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>is about liberation or freedom from the conditioning or from the known\".</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LiSNiTBw45U/TiZPbY75yDI/AAAAAAAAEFQ/4ANePcAE9Sk/s1600/imagesCA05ISC4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"77\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LiSNiTBw45U/TiZPbY75yDI/AAAAAAAAEFQ/4ANePcAE9Sk/s400/imagesCA05ISC4.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">\"&nbsp;Unlearn what is learned and have outlived its relevance , so that you are open to learning 'what is unknown' . Your ability to open your future will depend not on how well you can learn anymore but also on how well you are able to unlearn. It is about letting go what has already been learnt acquired, and served you will for long. In your business you must keep away from workplace folks who are as consistant as an irresponsible ass\u201d. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7cVSPns41hU/TiZPiuHAClI/AAAAAAAAEFU/pdURDkaT4jk/s1600/imagesCAJKMPT7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7cVSPns41hU/TiZPiuHAClI/AAAAAAAAEFU/pdURDkaT4jk/s400/imagesCAJKMPT7.jpg\" width=\"259\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Seeing him UNUSUALLY receptive I continued \u2013 the gist is here --</span><br />\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Throughout our lives, we have all been plied with misinformation by the dominant culture, some of which has become internalized and become the gospel . We invented this software , so we know more than you-- Blah Blah\u2014</span><br />\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Unlearning things that are no longer useful can be an extreme form of changing, like an almost physical casting off of inner clothing.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Unlearning involves a conscious individual confrontation of the past with the future, involving paradigms or beliefs that come from the fully formed past at odds with those that come from a future, still in formation. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-x08iFuAfnDg/TiZPo8luF8I/AAAAAAAAEFY/IzOyZWuWhI8/s1600/imagesCAYSF1JO.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-x08iFuAfnDg/TiZPo8luF8I/AAAAAAAAEFY/IzOyZWuWhI8/s320/imagesCAYSF1JO.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">The risk, the vulnerability of not having answers, of being in-between ideas, of acting in the face of the unknown, has to be faced as unlearning takes place. In this way unlearning prepares the ground for a deeper kind of learning.</span><br />\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Unlearning is NOT the opposite of learning. It is about letting go old outdated knowledge . If you need to fill up water in a bottle, the ( hot ) air which served the bottle well for long time, must be allowed to escape. Unlearning is about moving away from something rather than moving towards something.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8IZlM-B_toU/TiZPuoZLYSI/AAAAAAAAEFc/PKqaKijE8qo/s1600/imagesCAPKN72C.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"295\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8IZlM-B_toU/TiZPuoZLYSI/AAAAAAAAEFc/PKqaKijE8qo/s400/imagesCAPKN72C.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Almost every day you will need to sweep the corners of your mind and consider what you need to UNLEARN and recast your mind. Learning technology has brought you to this point of your life, only unlearning methodology will take you smoothly forward. You must have the courage and mental fortitude to rip apart every standard operation procedure manual of your company. There can be NO finality in any rethink. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">The whole world has been harping about Dec 21<span style=\"font-size: small;\"><sup>st</sup> 2012. This date is the start of the beginning of a new DNA programming age of \u201c Knowledge adds, wisdom subtracts\u201d . </span></span><br />\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Unlearning is not about right or wrong. It is about being open to and exploring something that lies underneath the judgment, underneath the right and the wrong.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZQbmdbMMRWI/TiZP1_ZAsdI/AAAAAAAAEFg/0YJUFbHFg08/s1600/imagesCAWW1BX7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZQbmdbMMRWI/TiZP1_ZAsdI/AAAAAAAAEFg/0YJUFbHFg08/s400/imagesCAWW1BX7.jpg\" width=\"311\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Becoming creative is an unlearning rather than a learning process ... because it gives the short end of the stick to existing moronic assumptions</span><br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\">A change mentor that infuriates your ego rather than soothes it, can speed up the process of unlearning.</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">You first need to unlearn your pre-conceived notion of what's achievable, and what is the need of the hour. The illiterate of the future are not those that cannot read or write. They are those that can not learn, <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">unlearn</span>, relearn.<span class=\"MsoHyperlink\"><span style=\"color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;\">\u2014and who are die hard supporters of the dog eared standard operations book.</span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sDbIyPA0oFo/TiZP-gMztcI/AAAAAAAAEFk/NWByp6MQzmU/s1600/imagesCAOV74ZP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sDbIyPA0oFo/TiZP-gMztcI/AAAAAAAAEFk/NWByp6MQzmU/s1600/imagesCAOV74ZP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-style: normal;\">In a time of drastic change, it is the unlearners who inherit the future. The learned find themselves equipped to live in a world that has ceased to exist. Imagine a computer engineer who cannot unlearn.</span></em></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">The learning cycle, which should be a virtuous circle that positively feeds itself. Instead it becomes a standard operation stuck record with the same lessons being learnt time and time again, without leading to any significant shifts or changes in practice.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Unlearning as the process of letting go of what is or what is known, in order to create fresh space for new learning to take root.. </span></span><br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><br /></span></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NIbq_ARpJ6o/TiZQHf9uIXI/AAAAAAAAEFo/84YIukcWStg/s1600/imagesCA81KI9L.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"258\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NIbq_ARpJ6o/TiZQHf9uIXI/AAAAAAAAEFo/84YIukcWStg/s400/imagesCA81KI9L.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">You had once asked me why Cornell loves to make you do <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>NLP/ AskMSR critiques. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>In its debative mode say of a scientific critique, disproving as a form of unlearning, injects a rigour and discipline into enquiry, and huge excitement. Unlearning is however a challenge. Truth that we can work with, not to test or to pass judgement but to help bring consciousness so that the next step can be taken.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">What might have once been a healthy, regular monthly review, can become a tiresome disconnected ritual that has lost its point or focus. Our habit of planning <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>in a particular way may have to worked wonderfully well in the past, but unknown to us, it has become a primary cause of our inability to adapt to changes in our context. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Even in mild <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>forms, these habits can become ingrained, comfort zones, addictions, hiding places of denial and self-protection. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-uE8SZABKZak/TiZQPNhokRI/AAAAAAAAEFs/-oUoUA5jkes/s1600/imagesCAXFKSQ5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"292\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-uE8SZABKZak/TiZQPNhokRI/AAAAAAAAEFs/-oUoUA5jkes/s400/imagesCAXFKSQ5.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Like a wheel-rut on a dirt road, and bosses who have bedded down for retirement, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>resist like hell, efforts to break out despite the fact that consciously the need is crystal clear.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Often our ability to see something, to appreciate its true nature, is skewed or hidden by the judgement we give it, the pigeon-hole we have prepared for it.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It is a uphill task to make them appreciate the need to just see something without judgement or assumption <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>.Old ingrained habits that do not serve us take time to break and some may never be broken.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Behind the fears live the memories that gave rise to them . The cat who fell in hot water is circumspect with cold water too. We cannot disprove our past or invalidate our memories. We go back and work gently with what happened, see the memories afresh and hopefully find the strength necessary to free ourselves from their power.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">It is painful to unlearn those deep, hidden and sometimes painful patterns that mask and influence the way we do things. Beginning at about 50 kilometres and extending above 1,000 kilometres with a maximum at 400 kilometres, the ionosphere is formed primarily by the action of sunlight on atmospheric particles. There, sunlight strips electrons from neutral atoms and produces a partially ionized gas (plasma). On the dayside of the Earth near local noon and near the subsolar point, the Sun heats the ionosphere to high temperatures and causes it to flow away from noon toward midnight in a roughly radial pattern. The flow moves both neutral atoms and charged particles across the Earth's magnetic field lines. <br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hDCtybs4cH0/TiLnaBzhEkI/AAAAAAAAEA8/hrxHEKZAkys/s1600/imagesCAVZ9J6U.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"239\" m$=\"true\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hDCtybs4cH0/TiLnaBzhEkI/AAAAAAAAEA8/hrxHEKZAkys/s320/imagesCAVZ9J6U.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe Lorentz force causes the charges to be deflected in opposite directions perpendicular to the velocity of the charges and also the local field. This charge separation creates an electric field that also exerts a force on the charged particles. The form of the resulting electric field distribution is strongly dependent on the distribution of ionospheric conductivity and magnetic field. There is little ionospheric conductivity on the nightside and hence no current can flow there. As for the magnetic field, it points upward in the Southern Hemisphere, horizontally northward at the Equator, and downward in the Northern Hemisphere. The horizontal component of the magnetic field exerts a vertical force on charges that move as a result of winds. At the Equator this causes the positive and negative charges to be deflected vertically and produces a strong vertical electric field that impedes further separation of the charges. At higher magnetic latitudes, the magnetic field is primarily vertical and the deflections are horizontal, producing horizontal electric fields.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ySHVtcmPXRc/TiLnlBC6PhI/AAAAAAAAEBA/_Xk3ebHfS9Q/s1600/imagesCATAI0FT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" m$=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ySHVtcmPXRc/TiLnlBC6PhI/AAAAAAAAEBA/_Xk3ebHfS9Q/s1600/imagesCATAI0FT.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn general, charges separated by mechanical or chemical forces, as in dynamos or batteries, will discharge if there is an external electrical conductor through which they can flow. They were like WOW1<br />\n<br />\nI told them what they saw was an actual&nbsp;SINK HOLE in Papau New Guinea, where my ship traded. &nbsp;I have been almost all over Papaua new Guinea--Port Moresby, Rabaul, Kimbe, Lae, Madang, Alotau, Wewak, Kavieng etc. In fact in that particular sinkhole there were deadly snakes, which the movie unit never saw, and hence they are lucky. Usually such Cobras, protect diamonds .<br />\n<br />\nThen my younger son aked me, \" Which is the most famous&nbsp;sink hole in the world?\"<br />\n<br />\nI said \" Without doubt , it is under the Egyptian Sphinx-- this planet does NOT know about it yet. Sinkholes can travel thousands of miles , especially if ann underground river exists. In the past there used to be the UNDERGROUND river Nile.
